//===WELCOME TO THE REALM KNOWN AS ZOMO'S BATTLECHIP FACTORY, ENJOY YOUR STAY===//

Actor BaseChip : CustomInventory //ALWAYS MAKE NEW CHIPS INHERIT FROM THIS
{
inventory.amount 1
inventory.maxamount 1
inventory.pickupmessage "You got a useless Battlechip... How did you get this?"
inventory.icon "WEAPQ0"
Inventory.PickupSound "item/1up"
scale 2.0
+INVENTORY.UNDROPPABLE
+COUNTITEM
+INVBAR
states
{
Spawn:
WEAP Q 5
loop
Use:
TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("DarkSoulFlag",1,"No")
TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("UsingSlot1",1,"GiveSlot1")
TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("UsingSlot2",1,"GiveSlot2")
TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("UsingSlot3",1,"GiveSlot3")
goto GiveSlot1
GiveSlot1:
TNT1 A 0
stop
GiveSlot2:
TNT1 A 0
stop
GiveSlot3:
TNT1 A 0
stop
No:
TNT1 A 0
fail
}
}

Actor ReshuffleChip : CustomInventory
{
inventory.amount 1
inventory.maxamount 1
inventory.pickupmessage "You got the Shuffle ability!"
inventory.icon "SHFLI0"
Inventory.PickupSound "item/1up"
Tag "Chip Shuffle"
scale 2.0
+INVENTORY.UNDROPPABLE
+COUNTITEM
+INVBAR
states
{
Spawn:
SHFL I 5
loop
Use:
TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("DarkSoulFlag",1,"No")
TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CustomAmmo",300,"Reshuffle")
fail
Reshuffle:
TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("CustomAmmo",350)
TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("Recover300Chip",99)
TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("FlashBombChip",99)

TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("YellowAppleChip",99)
TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("TimeBombChip",99)

Actor PADecider : ReshuffleChip
{
+INVENTORY.AUTOACTIVATE
States
{
Use:
TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"Advance1","Advance2","Advance3","Advance4","Advance5","Advance6","Advance7")
goto Advance1
Advance1:
TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ZomoUltHandler",0,1)
stop
Advance2:
TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ZomoUltHandler",0,2)
stop
Advance3:
TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ZomoUltHandler",0,3)
stop
Advance4:
TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ZomoUltHandler",0,4)
stop
Advance5:
TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ZomoUltHandler",0,5)
stop
Advance6:
TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ZomoUltHandler",0,6)
stop
Advance7:
TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ZomoUltHandler",0,7)
stop
No:
TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("misc/clnbell","Voice")
stop
}
}

Actor ShuffleItem : CustomInventory
{
inventory.amount 1
inventory.maxamount 1
inventory.pickupmessage "You got the Shuffle Item!"
inventory.icon "SHFLI0"
Inventory.PickupSound "item/1up"
scale 2.0
+INVENTORY.UNDROPPABLE
+COUNTITEM
+INVBAR
states
{
Spawn:
SHFL I 5
loop
Pickup:
TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ZomoChipShuffle",0)
stop
}
}
